        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2198911566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8662241169877659823">This review originally appeared on <a href='https://brizzlelassbooks.com/2017/12/12/review-you-had-me-at-hello-by-mhairi-mcfarlane/' rel='nofollow noopener'>BrizzleLass Books</a>.<br/><br/>It becomes clear with this book very quickly what the state of play is. Rachel and Ben are best friends through Uni but there are very definitely underlying feelings there between them. The problem Rachel is in a long-term relationship. When they go their separate ways at the end of Uni their friendship falls apart and ten years later bump into each other reigniting their friendship and those old feelings, except this time Ben is married.<br/><br/>While</span>
  <span id="freeText8662241169877659823" style="display:none">This review originally appeared on <a href="https://brizzlelassbooks.com/2017/12/12/review-you-had-me-at-hello-by-mhairi-mcfarlane/" rel="nofollow noopener">BrizzleLass Books</a>.<br /><br />It becomes clear with this book very quickly what the state of play is. Rachel and Ben are best friends through Uni but there are very definitely underlying feelings there between them. The problem Rachel is in a long-term relationship. When they go their separate ways at the end of Uni their friendship falls apart and ten years later bump into each other reigniting their friendship and those old feelings, except this time Ben is married.<br /><br />While the story was easy to read, and emotionally charged throughout I just didn’t connect to either of the characters in the way I would have liked. I found them both a little self-serving and immature. While the outcome is pretty much a given in these books I was hoping they would walk away lonely and apart because I didn’t think they deserved each other, they didn’t deserve that love or even wanted it enough.<br /><br />This was a fail for me, I didn’t enjoy the characters, every single person in this book is out for themselves, there is a definite lack of human compassion here. I found the plot predictable and unoriginal and I didn’t connect with the writing style at all.</span>

<div id="review_939518163" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/939518163" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/939518163?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=stand-alone-novel">stand-alone-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=womens-fiction-chicklit">womens-fiction-chicklit</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer939518163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13834832214350210897"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15733851.You_Had_Me_At_Hello' title='You Had Me At Hello by Mhairi McFarlane' rel='nofollow noopener'>You Had Me At Hello</a> is a standalone novel written by author <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6434584.Mhairi_McFarlane' title='Mhairi McFarlane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mhairi McFarlane</a>. This was a great book and it actually held a lot of humor which I really enjoyed. It centers on the topic of "the one that got away". Rachel and Ben were best friends that could have been much, much more. Now, a decade later, they find each other again kinda-sorta by chance. This is not a mindless chick-lit book where everything falls into place easily with a happily ever after. Rather it shows the reality of ten years</span>
  <span id="freeText13834832214350210897" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15733851.You_Had_Me_At_Hello" title="You Had Me At Hello by Mhairi McFarlane" rel="nofollow noopener">You Had Me At Hello</a> is a standalone novel written by author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6434584.Mhairi_McFarlane" title="Mhairi McFarlane" rel="nofollow noopener">Mhairi McFarlane</a>. This was a great book and it actually held a lot of humor which I really enjoyed. It centers on the topic of "the one that got away". Rachel and Ben were best friends that could have been much, much more. Now, a decade later, they find each other again kinda-sorta by chance. This is not a mindless chick-lit book where everything falls into place easily with a happily ever after. Rather it shows the reality of ten years later and the lives lived by two people who went their separate ways. As we see Rachel and Ben reunite in the present, we also learn the nature of their relationship back in their university days and what happened right before the ten-year gap. When I realized that this was not an easy fairytale type book, I honestly had no idea how the story would end. Needless to say, as a reader who connected and understood all the characters involved, I was happy with the proposed ending. In addition to Rachel and Ben's interactions, there are some other sub-plots and side characters that add additional layers to this story. It is an entertaining read and I would recommend it. I thoroughly enjoyed it.<br /><br />As a person in a committed relationship, this book made me think. What good can really come of seeking out former flames "just to say hi". It is only human to wonder "What if?" but there is also danger in that thought process. Regret steals our present-day joy and life is much too short for that. I really connected with a quote in this book: "I don't expect to be happy ever after. Just happier' 'But it all comes down to what we call happy. I think we're the generation that's spent too much time thinking about what we haven't got instead of what we do have."<br /><br /><b>My favorite quote:</b><br /><i>“When you love someone, you want their happiness even when it's not going to involve you. Even when it depends on your lack of involvement."</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13834832214350210897" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_496078414" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/496078414" />
    <a title="Zanna Mackenzie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10703273-zanna-mackenzie"><img alt="Zanna Mackenzie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442875609p2/10703273.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/496078414?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zanna Mackenzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zanna Mackenzie" href="/user/show/10703273-zanna-mackenzie">Zanna Mackenzie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10703273-zanna-mackenzie?shelf=my-favourite-books">my-favourite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer496078414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10699040803250114458">Everyone seems to have raved about this debut novel and I can now see why. I took the, for me, very unusual step of reading the last chapter first with this book because I just knew reading it any other way would drive me crazy and I'd be trying to read it so fast to find out what happened that I'd not take in all the details of the story. As it turned out reading the last chapter first didn't help matters. As the story of Rachel and Ben unfolded I just kept reading and reading, knowing how the </span>
  <span id="freeText10699040803250114458" style="display:none">Everyone seems to have raved about this debut novel and I can now see why. I took the, for me, very unusual step of reading the last chapter first with this book because I just knew reading it any other way would drive me crazy and I'd be trying to read it so fast to find out what happened that I'd not take in all the details of the story. As it turned out reading the last chapter first didn't help matters. As the story of Rachel and Ben unfolded I just kept reading and reading, knowing how the book ended but desperate to know how it all came about. Usually I'm not a fan of flashbacks in novels but in this case I couldn't get to the flasback sections fast enough, so keen was I to learn a little more about Ben and Rachel and their past.<br /><br />The charcaters in this book feel like real friends and Ben and Rachel are wonderfully written; Ben especially. I read late into the night last night and then started reading again over my breakfast today and didnt stop until I'd finished! I so wanted to finish the book but at the same time I felt great sadness when I did - simply because it was such a good story and the characters so likeable that I felt sorry at not being in 'their world' anymore.<br /><br />Buy the book, read it, I don't think you'll regret it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10699040803250114458" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_458511619" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458511619" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7014707-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346106160p2/7014707.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458511619?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/7014707-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/16050702-you-had-me-at-hello">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458511619" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2311161787202944115">A really good read, Mhairi writes with a style that absorbs you into the story, I really enjoyed the way that that story was told both from the present, but also with insights into the past, and what made them who they were in the present.<br/><br/>There were many ways that the story could have gone, I knew the outcome I wanted but could so easliy see many different twists.<br/><br/>A definate author that I'm going to look out for.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

Which was so so part of the fun. <br/><br/>Btw, I LOVE the narrator's voice but didn't work out to listen as much as I would have liked, so mostly print for this one. 3.5, rounding up.</span>

    <a title="Amanda McGill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32377593-amanda-mcgill"><img alt="Amanda McGill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511788919p2/32377593.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3359500907?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda McGill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda McGill" href="/user/show/32377593-amanda-mcgill">Amanda McGill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32377593-amanda-mcgill?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3359500907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7059860985346399589">Such a perfect summertime (or COVID escape) read! <br/><br/>I really enjoyed the two main characters, Rachel and Ben, and reading about their story. The novel goes back and forth between the present day, where Rachel and Ben see each other for the first time since university graduation, and 13 years ago when they were best friends in university. I liked the friendship between the two of them and was curious on what was going to happen. <br/><br/>The novel did have different subplots going on and while I appreciated</span>
  <span id="freeText7059860985346399589" style="display:none">Such a perfect summertime (or COVID escape) read! <br /><br />I really enjoyed the two main characters, Rachel and Ben, and reading about their story. The novel goes back and forth between the present day, where Rachel and Ben see each other for the first time since university graduation, and 13 years ago when they were best friends in university. I liked the friendship between the two of them and was curious on what was going to happen. <br /><br />The novel did have different subplots going on and while I appreciated that this wasn't just an one plot story, I did find that the novel dragged in the middle and pages could of been cut to have the story more tight. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7059860985346399589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kP45i7FhXvrrrLv8p2OiXjTf7c9LBINjrjlEca4qE50QP3T5Od0fYCmqGB9ACeTUpF9gVPs9ew8Dc1ze8/i30Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eOFscbiudnVRXoiKFRWoVjUmCKkWAW4K3HvXBRAiIo/4ICEDMBI375NYK2nyf+7cpaaFMqY4lmZxMc+qTfCGww==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14553915951485144458">Mhairi was born in Scotland in 1976 and her unnecessarily confusing name is pronounced Vah-Ree.<br/><br/>After some efforts at journalism, she started writing novels. It’s Not Me, It’s You is her third book. She lives in Nottingham, with a man and a cat.</span>
